New Delhi, Apr.10 (ANI): Expressing grave concern over the loss of innocent lives following the massive fire at the Puttingal temple in Kerala&#x27;s Kollam district, Congress veteran and former defence minister A.K. Antony on Sunday said that this untoward incident should not be politicised and demanded a thorough investigation into the matter so that the perpetrators are brought to book. My sympathies are with families who have been affected by this,&quot; Antony told ANI. Meanwhile, the Congress Party has said the Kerala Government has decided to order a judicial enquiry into the tragic incident, adding that anyone found guilty would be suitably punished.</p>
